- 2 chiles guajillos

- aguacate al gusto
- tostadas al horno

Se pones en agua con sal los chiles y el ajo a hervir.  Ya que estén suaves se enjuagan y se les quitan las semillas. Se pasan a la licuadora con un poco de caldo, sazonar con orégano, sal de mar y pimienta.  En una olla ponemos un poquito de aceite de oliva y guisamos la salsa unos 2 minutos.  Agregan el resto del caldo y dejan hervir, rectificar sazón y agregar las verduras (calabaza, chayote, zanahorias) picadas.  Se dejan por 10 minutos o hasta que estén suaves.  Para servir agregan lechuga, rábanos, chile y aguacate.  Acompañar con tostadas 😋. #freshbitesana #vegan #meatlessmonday #healthylunch #healthyrecipes #lunessincarne #organic #glutenfree #realfood #eatclean #recetassaludables #motivación #ideas #foodie"

In honor of #WorldWildlifeDay yesterday, Kenya's President Uhuru Kenyatta got #seriousaboutwildlifecrime. Taking a positive anti-poaching stand, he burned 15 tons of ivory. 
#DSWT founder Dr. Dame Daphne Sheldrick DBE shared her thoughts on the ceremony: "We stood in awe as this funeral pyre of confiscated ivory from numerous elephants went up in flames while the moon rose behind. We contemplated if, amidst this heap, lay the tusks from some of our orphans' lost mothers, and of all those magnificent lives lost. We reflected on the herds that this represented, that should still be alive, and not lost forever, but better their ivory be burnt to dust today so that it can never have economic value on someone's mantel piece tomorrow. We are immensely proud today of Kenya's stand."
